Unfortunately, Subpart D, âWalking-Working Surfaces,â has provided little in the way of clear, concise requirements. According to the FMCSA, safety can be achieved within your organization by putting this model in place. In fact, the agency recently trained 1000+ Federal and State Partner employees on this improved investigative process. The SMC moves beyond identifying what the safety violation is to why the safety performance issue is occurring so motor carriers can develop or refine policies, practices and operations to improve their safety performance. \n\nThis webcast shows how to enhance efficiencies and reduce costs and fines\n\t\t          </div>\n\t\t          <div class=\"event-cta\">\n\t\t          \t\n\t\t            <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://jjkeller.adobeconnect.com/e4zrt0y5beq/event/registration.html?campaign-id=NPTC\">Register Now!</a>\n\t\t          </div>\n\t\t        </div>\n\t\t      </div>\n\t\t    \n\t\t      <div class=\"event-item-container clear-fix\">\n\t\t        <div class=\"event-date-container\">\n\t\t          \n\t\t          <div class=\"event-date-start\">\n\t\t            <a href=\"/learn/events#event42\">Jul 13</a>\n\t\t          </div>\n\t\t          \n\t\t            <div class=\"event-time-container\">\n\t\t              <div class=\"event-time-start\">\n\t\t                <a href=\"/learn/events#event42\">10:00AM</a>\n\t\t              </div>\n\t\t              <div class=\"event-time-end\">\n\t\t                <a href=\"/learn/events#event42\">#event42\"&gt;11:00AM</a>\n\t\t              </div>\n\t\t            </div>\n\t\t  \t  \t           \n\t\t        </div>\n\t\t        <div class=\"event-details-container\">\n\t\t          <div class=\"event-title\">\n\t\t            <a href=\"/learn/events#event42\">Roadside Inspections</a>  \n\t\t          </div>\n\t\t          <div class=\"event-type\">\n\t\t            Webcasts - \n\t\t          </div>\n\t\t          <div class=\"event-summary\">\n\t\t            Vehicle inspections make good sense, but are also required under law. A regimen of a complete pre-trip at the beginning of the day, walk-around inspection every time the vehicle is parked, and a post-trip at the end of the day is the best practice. Drivers also need to know what to check on the vehicle and how to spot defects, who to call when there is a problem, and how and when to submit documentation. This, coupled with a competent maintenance department or service, helps keep vehicles on the road in good shape while maintaining low CSA BASIC scores. \n\nThis webcast reviews critical information and understanding about: performing vehicle inspections; filing out vehicle inspection forms; the consequences of a roadside DOT inspection; protecting equipment, and upholding a driver and organizationâs reputation.\n\t\t          </div>\n\t\t          <div class=\"event-cta\">\n\t\t          \t\n\t\t            <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://jjkeller.adobeconnect.com/e1s7qowkn8k/event/registration.html?campaign-id=JJKeller.com\">Register Now!</a>\n\t\t          </div>\n\t\t        </div>\n\t\t      </div>\n\t\t    \n\t\t      <div class=\"event-item-container clear-fix\">\n\t\t        <div class=\"event-date-container\">\n\t\t          \n\t\t          <div class=\"event-date-start\">\n\t\t            <a href=\"/learn/events#event43\">Jul 25</a>\n\t\t          </div>\n\t\t          \n\t\t            <div class=\"event-time-container\">\n\t\t              <div class=\"event-time-start\">\n\t\t                <a href=\"/learn/events#event43\">9:30AM</a>\n\t\t              </div>\n\t\t              <div class=\"event-time-end\">\n\t\t                <a href=\"/learn/events#event43\">#event43\"&gt;2:30PM</a>\n\t\t              </div>\n\t\t            </div>\n\t\t  \t  \t           \n\t\t        </div>\n\t\t        <div class=\"event-details-container\">\n\t\t          <div class=\"event-title\">\n\t\t            <a href=\"/learn/events#event43\">Practical Guidance for ELog Success: From Ideas to Plan</a>  \n\t\t          </div>\n\t\t          <div class=\"event-type\">\n\t\t            Executive Seminars - Tampa, FL\n\t\t          </div>\n\t\t          <div class=\"event-summary\">\n\t\t            Fleets with drivers who currently use paper logs need to transition their drivers to electronic logs by December 18, 2017.
